<span style="font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">- Likhonin: All of Russia will go crazy</span><span style="font-weight: normal;font-style: normal;text-decoration: none;background-color:rgb(30, 30, 30);color:rgb(255, 255, 255);"> <span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">as soon as they read it. </span><p></p><p style="font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30);"><span style="font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Russia, the people, the intellectuals.
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
All they can do is shout and swear among themselves, 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
but they themselves do not understand anything, 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
because Russia and her people live by their own laws. 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
And not by the laws that the eggheads in the capital write. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Therefore, I would like to drink now to my friend, to my spiritual mentor. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
I would even say, to a living classic, 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
to Sergey Ivanovich Platonov. Hooray!
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov: By the way, what are you calling you book?
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Likhonin: He's not just wise, he is a sage. 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
He does not try to preach to people, 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
he simply writes about the ills of society. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
For, here it is gentlemen - life, with all its ulcers. 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
With all its foul stenches, here it is, as it is. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
And you can draw your own conclusions.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov: What is the book about?
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Likhonin: Have you not read it yet? 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Why, Sergei Ivanovich Platonov, wrote about them.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov: What? You mean, about prostitutes?
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Likhonin: About this establishment.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov: What's your name again, Sergey?
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Platonov: Sergey Ivanovich Platonov.
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov: Sorry, but this isn’t serious at all. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
In fact, it’s downright funny.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Platonov: Do you think so?
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Zhenya: Don't throw your pearls before swine. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Here's today’s trouble - because of a wave of cheap public, 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
poor Pasha has been taken into a room more than ten times today 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
and every time by a different man.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Just now she had a hysterical fit and passed out. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Then, immediately after she came back to her senses, 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
they gave her a glass of alcohol with valerian drops 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
and Emma Eduardovna sent her out into the hall again. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
I tried to stand up for her, 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
but that housekeeper cursed at me and threatened to punish me.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov: What is she going on about?
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Zhenya: Don’t worry your head over it ... nothing important ... 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
just ... some of our little family's nonsense ...
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Zhenya: Sergey Ivanovich, can I have your wine?
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
It’s not worth it, Sergey Ivanovich. Don't bother …
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Platonov: Why not? I will do a very simple and innocent thing,
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
I will bring Pasha here, and if I must, I will pay for her. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Let's let her lie down here on the couch and have a little rest ... 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Go get Pasha.</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
- Sabashnikov; Yeah ... I guess you are a hero,
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
since they talk about you with such gasps of admiration. 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Vasily here is a simple man. Today he picked up a book and
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
discovered that the author is a genius. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
You know, tomorrow he'll pick up another book and 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
he'll send the previous genius to hell, 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
and he'll argue with all the scholars who oppose him 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
until he’s red in the face. He himself is a scholar, but a talentless one.
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Be quiet! I listened to you; I did not interrupt.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
He hasn't lifted a finger in his life to do anything. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
His father sends him money once a month. And he goes on:
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
“Oh, Dostoevsky. Oh, Kropotkin. Oh Gorky!"… 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
But only Gorky did not invite him to a brothel. 
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
Platonov invited him, so Platonov is a genius. 
</span><br>
<br><br><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><img src="images/x.gif"></span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
And he wrote about prostitutes, this whole thing is simply absurd.
</span><br><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
